Beautiful and well maintained golf course in Friant, CA. Golf Carts have on-board GPS touchscreen and they even give you bottled water on the carts. Staff is very friendly and professional. Price is reasonable and thank you for giving out military/veterans discounts!! Such a wonderful experience playing this outstanding golf course! Found another one of my favorites!<//text>

<Pics>None< /Pics>< Text>
Maybe the best course in central California.  Typical Johnny Miller course - a lot of variety (no two holes a like) and large, spralling, undulating greens.  And the crew keeps it in very good condition.

Anyone from a 30 to a single digit handicap index will enjoy this course.  But beware, you need to hone your putting skills, both in stroke/distance control, and in green reading.  (The first time I played this course I wanted to shoot bogey golf so badly.  Shot a 91...with 43 putts!I had so much fun, and was so frustrated at the same time.  Great day!)

The changes in elevation make this course sooooo much fun.  And yes, you cn loose golf balls here if you can't keep it close ot the fairway, but I can't think a another course in the area that offers so many different looks and such wonderful shot-making risk-reward opportunities.</Text>

< text>
Play golf here regularly, 3-4 times a week. Staff is very friendly and helpful, food in our restaurant is always very good, especially on Friday - clam chowder! The course is very challenging, very few flat or level lies. Greens are difficult due to subtle slopes. Beautiful scenery and very different from your flat valley courses!< /text>

I had extensive work done today and the care and attention to detail was superlative. I am a huge sissy when it comes to dental work, so I was very grateful to have nitrous, as well as other options available. I am especially impressed with the practice's willingness to invest in new technology and ongoing training for their people. Everyone did an excellent job of explaining each step of the procedure and what sensations I should expect. They even try to make the place not sound and smell like a dental office, by playing real music and offering a loaf fresh bread when you're done. The restroom was spotless, had high end soaps and lotions, and listerine available...and they even spent the money for high quality cloth-like hand towels. Those details truly help set this practice apart. I also noticed a mild dress code, with hygienists and assistants in lab coats and front desk people in black tops, and everyone was well groomed and very professional in their appearance and demeanor - all of which I found incredibly refreshing. While I was in the chair, what I felt most was overwhelming gratitude for having such advanced technology and experienced dentists and staff available to me. I wish I had come here 15 years ago!<//text>

Great place to get shoes at! Needed some sneakers and socks and the prices are *very* cheap, I got some Champion sneakers for $30 and my friend got his for $25 - they're high quality and great for running. The customer service was great - they helped me find the shoes I needed and even checked inventory for a new pair of those shoes. < Text>
Odd, know I reviewed this location a long time ago, no idea where review went. So, would say this is the 2nd best Super King Market I know of. Santa Ana location is the best I've seen. Parking is okay, can be a bit of an issue getting into and out of the lot. Parking, entrance, aisles, restroom and checkout are all accessible. Produce, meat, deli, dry goods and dairy all have a great selection at a decent price. When this location first opened it was funny to see the locals buying cart loads of food cause they were all under the impression that these were temporary prices. The bakery like all locations is now gone, bummer, had great stuff.  Restrooms are good. Staff are nice, some are really helpful and friendly. Come here often, will continue to do so.</Text>

<resp>None</resp><review>Super King is the king of supermarkets. Comparing with the Big Chain supermarkets, this place is just as large or larger, has a variety of large sections with ton of different items that you would not find in regular grocery stores.
So many people shop from there that's why the items are always fresh and being replaced by a hi purchase turnover. They carry a lot of different vegetables and fruits that I have not even seen in other grocery stores. The great thing about it is the freshness and the quantity and the quality of the items being displayed.
They have an international section for Mexican, Middle Eastern, Asian, and other hard to find items in other grocery stores. Their Seafood and Meat butcher area is large and carry anything from fish to scallops to Lobster to crab legs to shrimp and variety a kind of steaks ground beef pork and so on. They have an International deli section that carries mates from different parts of the world like Italian mortadella Kalamata olives other Delicacies.  You can get a variety of cheeses as well in the deli area. The bakery carries all kinds of different breads cakes and other desserts.
They have a large liquor section carrying a large variety of beers to high-end expensive brandies and whiskeys. Their Checkers are always on an running people through just to get the crowd paying for their items so no wait unless it's a very busy time which usually is.
The best part of all of this is their prices. You can save anywhere from $50-$100 for a full basket of different items compared to  shopping at Big Chain grocery stores. You don't have to buy anything in bulk and prices are very reasonable.<//review></record></dataset><record>

Only place you can get corned beef year-round. The butcher's has phenomenal selection of meats and amazing prices. Produce section is huge, easily twice what you'd see at a national chain and a FRACTION of the prices.

Place is ALWAYS busy, so parking and navigating the other shoppers is just short of a demolition derby.

Two biggest complaints, and why they only get three stars:

1) They got rid of their shopping baskets, so now they only have shopping carts. So now, if you're only there for a few things, you still have to take a cart. This only exacerbates congestion.

2) Recently, they got rid of their baggers, so you have to bag your own groceries. They're a grocery store not a box store. It REALLY slows things down, and is an added burden for the elderly and handicapped. I was there assisting someone picking up a birthday cake. I was thoroughly impressed by their full bakery services. They have a very wide assortment of pastries, cakes, cupcakes, muffins, and cookies. All the items are baked and decorated on site.
